// Reactions added by A.G. Vandeputte for hydrogen abstraction from JP-10
// 5 new nodes were added October 22nd 
// 
// C/H2/NonDeC_5ring_fused6_1 : secondary C atom on a 5 ring, that is part of the fused 6 ring 
// C/H/Cs3_5ring_fused6 : tertiary C atom on a fused 5 + 6 ring, e.g. tertiary site of norbornane
// C/H2/NonDeC_5ring_fused6_2 : secondary C atom on a 5 ring, that is not part of the fused 6 ring
// C/H/Cs3_5ring_adj5 : tertiary C atom on a C atom that is part of two non-fused 5 rings
// C/H2/NonDeC_5ring_alpha6ring : secondary C atom on a 5 ring, in alpha of the flanking 6 ring (JP10)
// C/H2/NonDeC_5ring_beta6ring : secondary C atom on a 5 ring, in beta of the flanking 6 ring (JP10)
// Rate coefficients were obtained by calculating the habstractions involving methyl using BMK/cbsb7 with inclusion of HR
// CBS-QB3 GAV°´s were then used to estimate the rate coefficients with a variety of radical sites
//  
// Despite the fact they are not CBS-QB3 and use GA, I would give these a priority of 4. Aaron
//
